	"race_human_lore" "The Tau'ri were created by the Ancients, representatives of an ancient and incredibly advanced race, the fruits of the first evolution of people, who wanted to populate the Milky Way with intelligent life forms. However, the project was not completed, as the Ancients had to leave the planet due to an epidemic that broke out. After some time, the planet Tau'ri was found by the Supreme System Lord Ra, who seized power over the planet and, with the help of the Star Gate, spread the human race to many other planets."
	"race_spirits_lore" "Spirits are beings who came to Earth from another dimension. Their appearance is preceded by a “Spatial Rift”. Each spirit has different unique abilities - the Astral Robe and the Angel it summons. Some of them do not remember their past and why they appeared in this world."
	"race_armored_lore" "Military equipment is the technical means available to the armed forces and ensuring their combat operations and daily functioning. All technology uses energy as a resource to use abilities."

	"race_asgard_lore" "The Asgards are one of the most advanced modern alien civilizations. The Asgards treat people favorably and sometimes share their advanced technologies with them. Physiologically, representatives of this race are classic “gray men”, well known from science fiction."
	"race_ori_lore" "The Ori are an aggressive, religiously inclined faction of the Ancients that developed into an independent society after the Ancients fled their home galaxy. One of the most highly developed civilizations in the four known galaxies. They used self-confidence on other, “lower” beings to increase their strength."

<font color='#d63131ef'>Нет ограничения по времени</font><br><br>

Жажда странствий – это стандартная Молитва. Она не ограничена по времени. В рамках Молитвы доступны не эксклюзивные персонажи.<br><br>
За каждые 10 Молитв вы гарантированно получите как минимум одного персонажа 4★.<br><br>
※ При обычных условиях базовая вероятность выпадения всех персонажей распределяется равномерно. Если действуют какие-либо усиления или гарантии, пожалуйста, прочтите соответствующие правила.<br><br>
〓 Правила 〓<br>
Базовая вероятность получения героя 5★ = 1,600%. Гарантированное получение героя 5★ как минимум один раз за 90 попыток.<br><br>
Базовая вероятность получения героя 4★ = 13,100%. Гарантированное получение героя 4★ как минимум один раз за 10 попыток.<br><br>
Базовая вероятность получения героя 3★ = 85,300%.<br><br>

<font color='#c2133f'>Важно!<br>
Если при опросе вы указали негативное отношение к аниме тематике, то вам не будут выпадать персонажи данной категории!</font><br>

<br>〓 Дубликаты 〓<br><br>

		"gun_type_4_lore"					"Soviet heavy long-range gun from the Second World War. This gun was based on a modernized 122 mm gun of the 1931 model, with the barrel of the previous model 122 mm gun superimposed on the carriage of a 152 mm ML-20 howitzer gun. The gun was mass-produced from 1939 to 1946 and was actively and successfully used in the Great Patriotic War, forming, together with the ML-20, the basis of the powerful cannon artillery of the RVGK. After the end of the war, this artillery system was in service for a long time with the Soviet army and a number of other countries; in several countries they are still in use today. The most powerful serial tank guns of World War II were created on the basis of the gun. <br>"

		"reactions_des_0"															"Select your desired reaction from the list above."
		"reactions_des_1"															"Iron synthesis is a chain of reactions taking place under constantly increasing pressure inside a star, in which, due to the collision of nuclei of chemical elements heavier than neon with helium, increasingly heavier elements are synthesized, stopping at iron (due to the fact that it has the highest binding energy per nucleon in the nucleus, the synthesis of elements heavier than iron is thus impossible) (requires 30,000 energy, produces iron, necessary for some armor improvements)."
		"reactions_des_2"															"The triple alpha process is a chain of thermonuclear reactions in the interior of stars, during which three helium-4 nuclei form a carbon-12 nucleus. At high enough pressure, this cycle can continue with the synthesis of oxygen (requires a total of 12,000 units of energy, produces oxygen necessary for farming the absurd forest)."
		"reactions_des_3"															"Decay of uranium-238 (radium series, uranium cascade) - the naturally occurring cascade decay of the uranium-238 isotope nucleus into lighter elements with the emission of multiple alpha particles (generates 12,000 energy, produces polonium-210, necessary for some improvements to weapons, as well as lead-206, necessary for creating anti-radiation protection)."
		"reactions_des_4"															"A proton-proton chain is a set of thermonuclear reactions during which hydrogen is converted into helium in stars located on the main stellar sequence. This cycle can bring up to 98% of the total energy of the star (produces 32,000 units of energy)."
		"reactions_des_5"															"Decay of uranium-235 is a reaction of forced decay of uranium-235 under the influence of neutrons irradiating it, as a result of which the nucleus is divided into two fragments (strontium-90 and xenon-133) and 2 free neutrons are separated. Strontium-90, obtained in this reaction, is necessary as one of the components to obtain an anti-radiation protection complex for completing the final quest."
		"reactions_des_6"															"The production of cobalt-60 is the reaction of stable cobalt-59 with thermal neutrons, which results in the formation of the radioactive isotope cobalt-60, which is necessary as a catalyst for some decay reactions."
